<div>\n  It takes the brightest minds to be a technology leader. It takes imagination to create green energy for the generations to come. At Siemens Gamesa we make real what matters, join our global team.\n <\u002Fdiv>\n <div>\n   Siemens Gamesa Renewable Energy (SGRE) is world market leader in offshore wind power, and with our innovations SGRE aims to make the difference for wind power projects throughout the world. SGRE supplies wind turbines and is an outstanding supplier of reliable, environmentally friendly and affordable renewable energy systems. In 90 countries worldwide we supply clean and renewable energy in the form of wind turbines with a total capacity of 85 GW, of which 50 GW under service, and a team of 25.000 employees. Its end-to-end value chain presence encompasses onshore and offshore wind turbines design, manufacturing, installation as well as cutting-edge service solutions. Well-known projects in the Netherlands include the Gemini, Westermeerwind, Borssele 1-2 and Fryslân.\n <\u002Fdiv>\n <div><\u002Fdiv>\n <div>\n   For more information about our dynamic and rapidly expanding work environment check out the video's in the Siemens Gamesa section on YouTube.\n <\u002Fdiv>\n <div><\u002Fdiv>\n <div>\n   We are looking for a Trouble Shooter to join our Service team in Lemmer.\n <\u002Fdiv>\n <div><\u002Fdiv>\n <div>\n   What are the key responsibilities associated with the job?\n <\u002Fdiv>\n <div><\u002Fdiv>\n <div>\n   As Trouble Shooter you perform maintenance jobs, trouble shooting activities and resolve product issues for customer equipment. As a team lead you do this without supervision and are accountable for the safety, competency and productivity of Trainees, Maintenance technicians and Contractors assigned to you. You identify reoccurring faults on electrical and mechanical systems of the turbine. You develop and share advanced troubleshooting knowledge and skills with other technicians and trouble shooters. Providing on job qualification training, evaluating competency and quality for troubleshooting procedures of individuals assigned to them is part of the job. Of course you keep records, maintain documentation, follow safety procedures and report technical, safety issues and difficulties to the relevant individuals on site\u002Fback office. The working schedule varies per wind park from 4 days on\u002Foff (Lemmer) to even 1 or 2 weeks on\u002Foff (offshore). Also the transfer set up differs from a Crew Transfer Vessel (CTV) (Project Lemmer) to\u002Ffrom the turbines to a Service Operating Vehicle (SOV) (Project Gemini).\n <\u002Fdiv>\n <div>\n  <div>\n   <br> What do we offer?\n  <\u002Fdiv>\n  <div>\n   <div>\n    <br> A great place to work within a rapidly growing market. <div>\n  It takes the brightest minds to be a technology leader. It takes imagination to create green energy for the generations to come. At Siemens Gamesa we make real what matters, join our global team.\n <\u002Fdiv>\n <div>\n   In our Design Tools team we are looking for someone that will combine the responsibilities of a software developer and a process champion, hence someone who will coordinate and coach the software development team and contribute to the software development as well. For all our offshore wind farm projects, the department is responsible for performing site-specific wind turbine load calculations and support structure design, focusing on the primary (load carrying) structure. The Design Tools team is responsible for the development, maintenance and migration of the engineering software into a service-oriented cloud infrastructure. Important aspects of the software development are engineering process automation (e.g. structural load calculations) and user experience for more than a hundred engineers of various backgrounds. The team works in a DevOps environment to improve quality and feature delivery. The core team is situated in The Hague (NL) with collaborating members in USA, Denmark and India.\n <\u002Fdiv>\n <div><\u002Fdiv>\n <div>\n   What are the key responsibilities associated with the job?\n <\u002Fdiv>\n <div><\u002Fdiv>\n <div>\n  <i> Software Development Engineer<\u002Fi>\n <\u002Fdiv>\n <ul>\n  <li>\n   <div>\n     Assist the architect and senior developers in technical discussions within a digital transformation project merging the legacy system into a service orientated hybrid (micro-service) architecture;\n   <\u002Fdiv><\u002Fli>\n  <li>\n   <div>\n     Work with product owners to handle backlogs and new requests;\n   <\u002Fdiv><\u002Fli>\n  <li>\n   <div>\n     Join the development by hands on driving the software development and active sprint participation.
